<script type="text/javascript">


    var map;   
    var lastInfowindow = null;
    var checkMap = true;
    var loading = false;


    function checkShowMap(){
        if (checkMap == true) {
            if ( $(window).width() > 980 ){
                var scrollPosition = window.scrollY || window.pageYOffset;
                if (scrollPosition > $("#servizi-clienti").offset().top - $(window).height()) {
                    activeMap();
                }
            }else{
                $("#trova-agenzie .active-map").removeClass("hide");
                $("#trova-agenzie .icon-spinner-map").addClass("hide");
            }
        };
    }



    $(document).ready(function() {
        checkShowMap();
        var scrollTimerMap = null;
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if (scrollTimerMap) {
                clearTimeout(scrollTimerMap);   // clear any previous pending timer
            }
            scrollTimerMap = setTimeout(checkShowMap, 600);   // set new timer
        });

       
        $('.active-map').click(function(e) {
            activeMap();
        });


    }); 

    


    function activeMap(){

        $("#trova-agenzie .icon-spinner-map").removeClass("hide");        
        $("#trova-agenzie .active-map").hide();
        checkMap = false;
        loading = true;
        initMapHome();
        
        $(".icon-spinner-map").delay( 3000 ).fadeOut();
        $("#trova-agenzie .prelative").removeClass("hide");
    }

var marker_list = [];

    function initMapHome(){

        var center = new google.maps.LatLng(41.8919300, 12.5113300);    
        map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('map-all'), {
                center: center,
                zoom: 8,
                minZoom: 8,
                scrollwheel: false
              });

        var strictBounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds(
            new google.maps.LatLng(37.26,6.44),
            new google.maps.LatLng(46.90,18.46)
        );

        google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'dragend', function() {
        
            if (strictBounds.getNorthEast().lat() > map.getBounds().getNorthEast().lat() && strictBounds.getNorthEast().lng() > map.getBounds().getNorthEast().lng() && strictBounds.getSouthWest().lat() < map.getBounds().getSouthWest().lat() && strictBounds.getSouthWest().lng() < map.getBounds().getSouthWest().lng() ) return;
     
            var c = map.getCenter(),
                x = c.lng(),
                y = c.lat(),
                maxX = strictBounds.getNorthEast().lng(),
                maxY = strictBounds.getNorthEast().lat(),
                minX = strictBounds.getSouthWest().lng(),
                minY = strictBounds.getSouthWest().lat();
            
            if (x < minX) x = minX;
            if (x > maxX) x = maxX;
            if (y < minY) y = minY;
            if (y > maxY) y = maxY;
            
            map.setCenter(new google.maps.LatLng(y, x));
        });
